Three popular issuance mechanisms for Stablecoins today:\n\nIssued based on off-chain collateral mechanism. Typically, USDT issued by Tether Limited company commits that each USDT will be converted into 1 actual USD.\nIssued based on an on-chain collateral mechanism. On-chain collateral is locked on the blockchain, usually in a smart contract.
